<Rate>2</Rate>< review>
The actual gym itself is very nice, small, but functional and well kept.

Sadly I cannot in good consciousness actually recommend you go here. I had a 12 month contract that expired several months ago, yet I am still charged monthly. After they closed for a short time for COVID-19, the charges stopped, and I had assumed that was the end of them. Sadly now that they are reopened, the charges have started again.

Heed what other 1 and 2 star reviews tell you and stay away, there are better options in the area. They will fight with you both on the phone and in person that they cannot for some reason end your contract, giving excuse after excuse. I don't make very much money, and even their relatively small charges every month can be absolutely backbreaking.

To any employees of the business who choose to read this, I am setting up a flag with my bank to stop any future payments to your company.<//review>

< text>
Was in dire need for a Fro-yo fix. Decided to go to Bear Hugs for my first frozen yogurt in California. I‚Äôve been to several frozen yogurt places throughout Arizona before moving here, and I have to say that I loved going to Bear Hugs! The gentleman, possibly the owner, was friendly, courteous and super helpful. I was pleasantly surprised to see not only Frozen Yogurt and Sorbet but also Italian Ice and Gelato! The flavors were great and topping selection was right on point.

Also, decided to bring my boyfriend with me, because he had never had frozen yogurt before. He was extremely surprised at how much he enjoyed frozen yogurt instead of ice cream. We will definitely be returning and would recommend this for great Fro-yo.</text>

< Text>
Ridgecrest is definitely the last place on planet earth I would expect to see a frozen yogurt shop. And you'd think that a shop located in an area so far out into the middle of nothingness would play it safe with a selection of generic flavors, but the flavors they serve here are incredibly unusual, like peanut brittle and salted caramel and matcha green tea. I'd revisit if I ever had the misfortune of finding myself in Ridgecrest again.</Text>

<rate>1< /rate>< review>
If I could give this place zero stars, I would. I went here seeking medical care after I was robbed and assaulted. The specific service I was seeking was not available at this place and I was asked to wait to see a social worker who would refer me to a medical provider who could assist me with the very specific service I was seeking. I waited along with my sister to be called. I spoke with a nurse who directed me to move to a different waiting area. I waited some more. After nearly two hours waiting, I was finally called, my vitals signs were taken and I was informed my discharge papers would be ready soon. Huh? Accord to these people, they had paged me repeatedly and I never answered. My guess is that the nurse who directed me to wait at the other waiting room never informed or made a note to anyone that I had been asked to switch to a different location. Anyway, by this point, I was really upset and ready to leave and seek medical treatment elsewhere. The straw that broke the camel's back is the attitude of one of the nurses in particular who treated me like I was stupid and showed absolutely no empathy for my very delicate situation. If you enjoy being patronized, ignored, and being treated overall like you're insignificant, by all means go to this place. It's obvious they lack proper communication skills and their social skills are sub par.

UPDATE:

As of February 2020, I was billed almost 500 for a urine sample, and a blood sample for which I never received results or even know why they were taken. I also had my vital signs taken. At the time I received the bill, I only had about a week to make a payment. I didn't pay it since I didn't have the sum at hand and thought, I'll just pay when they send me the next reminder. Low and behold, I received the bill again and was dumbfounded to see that the amount due jumped to $1,413.30!!!!!!!!! That's right ladies and gentlemen, one grand for a urine sample, a blood sample and vitals. I almost feel like they should be paying ME for having made me waste my time. Ridiculous. I will contact the business manager who replied to my earlier review and see if they really are in the best disposition to be of assistance. I will update you all with honesty so you can make your own decision about whether you want to do business in a place like this or run for the hills--- I wish I had. The greed of the medical field is without bounds.

UPDATE 3/12/20: Called the number listed above--- and either they have lots of complaints or are otherwise "busy", as I have yet to hear from anyone. Also, the two bills referenced in the earlier update are TWO separate bills---- one for being in the emergency room (no mention of the services supposedly rendered), and a separate one for the medical attention I supposedly received from an MD and an NP (since when do MDs/NPs take vital signs and urine/blood samples? This is news to me, I only thought nurses or nurse assistants performed these functions. So either I'm being billed for services that never actually occurred or this great hospital is so innovative that its MDs and NPs are probably changing diapers and providing bedpans for ill patients). I called billing services and requested an ITEMIZED copy of the bills--- I also requested that the bills be audited to ensure that as an uninsured patient I am NOT being charged higher prices than insured patients---- which appears to be a normal practice in medical centers, so watch out if you're uninsured! I will update this review in the near future to inform anyone interested about how things are unfolding. I also plan to contact the BBB and if need by, the City Attorney.< /review>

< review>
Truly one of the worst places to be hospitalize. Sadly this place does not live up to its standards or even its own commitments. I say this as a past patient, a friend of past patients and currently a family member of a current patient. I have given many chances to this hospital to prove itself as a professional location and care unit but it has failed me time after time. The only way they help who they want to help. Countless times the ER staff is always talking about patients private info or they all all hanging around the registration window chit chatting away while people are trying to sign in. Then after sign in, the wait time is horrible, even if you have insurance. Once seen, the ball doesn't get rolling instead it comes to a halt. Waiting on nothing but endless test, and waiting on results. Test that you probably don't need but they refer to as, "procedure". You end up sleeping the night away waking up to a whole different staff who you once have to inform them why you are there and who you previously spoke and sign in with the previous night. Very unprofessional and in my opinion, "taking it back to the beginning of time". What is next? pencils and erasers in case they make medical prescription mistakes?
Once the whole ordeal of checking in and actually moving out of the ER into your own room ( may I add if your lucky to get a single because usually they are shared even if you request a single), you have to deal with a language barrier with practically 80% of the staff. Most are not even at a 5th grade level of basic English language. I speak English, Spanish and a bit Italian on a good day, but try those languages with them and your out of luck. After a whole day just to get in a bed, you once again have to go through a process of why you visited the location and whats wrong with you, what ever happen to all those test results?
Now, here is the worst part, if you want to believe there can possibly be any worst to this experiences. Try to call the hospital to speak to a family member, no seriously, try it. The constant back and forth and wrong information is ridiculous. They always blame the errors on the system or recent upgrades they had. Really? in one week you get 4 upgrades and no on knows how to use the system? After many years the story gets old. Then, once a complaint is made online, in the HR Dept. and over the phone to Supervisors, guess what? Nothing is done. I have not visited the hospital in a while as a patient, thank god. My current family members have but due to other reasons and location that is the only place, this is just a voice and experience. I can be judge or even hear all the opinion out there about this review but the experiences, my experiences and more are always repeated. Why? Can it be they don't fix matters, instead fix the front entrance and plant a tree and hang up stars and pictures instead and call it a day? Look for yourself.<//review>
